 *** Toyota Glanza ko bharat main launch kar diya gaya he
 Its starting price is 7
 22 lakh rupee (eks-showrooms, dilli) rakhi gai he
 At the same time, the price of its top variant is 8
 90 lakh rupee (eks-showrooms, dilli) tak rakhi gai he
 The Glanza car is the first car to be partnered by Maruti Suzuki and Toyota and is based on Maruti Suzuki's Baleno
 dizin ke maamle main Glanza or Baleno donon hi lagbhag ek jaisi hai
 Talking of change, Toyota badging will be seen in the grille, which is different in both cars
 Glanza ko do verients main pesh kiya gaya he, ye verients g or v hai
 In this, both automatic and manual transmission options will be available

 Let us know how page stress affects our everyday lives
 kis gun ke kaaran lamp kii batti main tel upar chadhataa he
 Some facts related to all of these important facts: Surface tension: Independent surface of the fluid has a tendency to get at least area, due to which its surface is always in a state of tension
 ise hi prishth tanaav kehete hai
 The surface tension of a fluid is the force that acts perpendicular to the line at the unit length of the imaginary line drawn on the surface of the fluid
 yadi rekha ki lambaai (l) par f bal kaary karata he, to prishth tanaav, t = f / l 
 s of page stress
 I
 The unit is newton / meter
 drav ke prishth ke kshetrafal main ekank vruddhi karne ke liye, kiya gaya kaary drav ke prishth tanaav ke baraabar hota he
 According to them, the unit of surface tension will be joule / meter ^ 2
 drav kaa taap badhaane par prishth tanaav kam ho jaataa he or kranthik taap (critical temp) par yah shunya ho jaataa he
 Cohesive force: The force of attraction between molecules of the same substance is called cohesive force
 thoson main sansanjak bal kaa maan adhik hota he, falswaroop unke aakaar nishchit hote hai
 The value of the cohesive force in gases is negligible
 aasanjak bal (adhesive force):do bhinn padaarthon ke anua ke madhya lagane vaale aakarshan-bal ko aasanjak bal kehete hai
 Due to adhesive force, one object sticks to another object
 keshikatv (capillarity tube):ek aisi khokhli nalee, jisaki trigya bahut kam tathaa ek samaan hoti he, kesanali kehalaata he
 The phenomenon of fluid over or under pressure in a capillary is called capillarity
 kis seemaa tak drav kesanali main chadhataa yaa utarataa he, yah kesanali kii trigya par nirbhar karata he
 The flow of fluid in the narrow tube is more and the flow of fluid in the wider tube is less
 saamanytah jo drav kaanch ko bhingota he, vah kesh nalee main upar chadh jaataa he, or jo drav kaanch ko nahi bhingota he vah neeche dab jaataa he
 For example, when the capillary is immersed in water, the water rises up and the surface of the water remains trapped inside the capillary
 iske vipareet kesanali ko jab paane main dubaaya jaataa he, to paara kesanali main bartan main rakhe paare kii sataha se neeche hi rahata he or kesanali main paara kii sataha ubhara hua rahata he
 Examples of capillarity: (i) Blotting absorbs paper-ink quickly, because the small holes in it act like capillaries
 (ii)laalaten yaa lamp kii batti main keshikatvan ke kaaran hi tel upar chadhataa he
 (iii) Water and essential salts reach the branches, stems and rows of plants and plants only through the action of capillarity
 (iv)kritrim upgrah ke andar (bharaheenta kii avasthaa) yadi kisi kesanali ko jal main khadaa kiya jaae to nalee main chadhane vaale jal stambh kaa prabhavi bhaar shunya hone ke kaaran jal nalee ke duusare sire tak pahunch jayega chaahe kesanali kitni bhi lambii kyon na ho
 (v) After rains, farmers plow their fields, so that the kestions created in the soil are broken and the water cannot come up and the soil can retain moisture

 reduce the surface tension of water, so they go deeper into the scum, which makes the cloth more clean

 " Political bills of CM Kejriwal on the electricity bill In comparison to other states, the electricity bill in Delhi is cheaper than the cost of less than 200 units
 In different states of power bill where there is an outcry over electricity prices, the days of Delhi people have come
 desh main aisa pehali baar ho rahaa he jab kisi rajya main bijli ke bill jiro aane lage hai
 Electricity is not only cheaper in Delhi than other states of the country, but now those who spend below 200 units are getting free electricity in the capital
 aagaamee dilli vidhansabha chunaav ke pehle arvind kejariwal ke jhole se dilli waalon ke liye lagaataar siyaasi saugat baras rahi he
 Mohammed Omar, who lives in Chiniot township of Paharganj, used to have electricity bill of between 400 and 500, but this time the electricity bill has also shocked him
 umr kehete hai, 'har baar bijli kaa bill 400 se 500 rupee aata tha, lekin is baar bijli kaa bill aayaa hi nahin he
 a total of seven electric appliances in Omar's home include fan fridge and light, but Mohammad Omar also understands the expensive political game behind cheap electricity
 umr kaa kahana he, 'pehle sasti mil rahi thi bijli par ab free mil rahi he, yah to badi acchhee baat he lekin asli niyat kya he yah to tab pataa chalegi jab dilli chunaav ke baad bhi bijli aisi hi sasti milti rahegi
 'other consumers who take advantage of free electricity live in their small house among the busiest markets in Sunil Karol Bagh
 ghar main do pankhaa, frij ke alaava zyada kuch nahin he
 a portion of the house is rented, but two separate meters of electricity are installed
 donon meter kaa bill unke phone par bisies kii ore se aa chukaa he or donon hi meter kaa bill jiro he
 Sunil says that his electricity bill used to come from 400 to 500 rupees every month, but this time he is happy with the zero electricity bill
 sunil ke mutabik unhen nahin pataa ki yah chunavi tohfa he yaa kejariwal sarkaar kii niyat, lekin philhal unako phayda hua he isliye ve khush hai
 In fact, Kejriwal started his politics with the issue of electricity, when in 2013 he opened a front against the then Chief Minister Sheila Dixit over the increased power prices
 bijli kii keemton ko waapas karwaane ke liye kejariwal anshan par baith gaye the
 Not only this, in the 2013 assembly elections Kejriwal appealed to the people not to fill up the increased electricity bills
 kai gharon ke conection jab bijli vibhaag dwaara kaat die gaye to kejariwal ne unke ghar jaakar apane haathon se taar jod diya tha
 50 per cent subsidy started In 2013, when Kejriwal won the election for the first time and became the Chief Minister for 49 days, he gave a 50% concession on electricity prices in Delhi within a week of joining the government
 2015 ke vidhansabha chunaav main jab kejariwal dobaaraa dilli kii satta main purna bahumat ke saath lautakar aae to unhone phir dilli waalon ke liye saugat dete hue apana vaada puraa kiya or 400 unit tak bijli kii keemton par 50 fisadi sabsidi kii shuruyaat kii
 Now before the 2020 assembly elections, Kejriwal gave free gifts of up to 200 units directly to Delhiites
 ghoshnaa ke ek maheene biit gaye or jaise hi logon ke bill aane shuru hue kisi ko yakeen nahin hua ki vaaki bijli ke bill jiro ho sakate hai
 That is, if you spend up to 200 units in Delhi, your electricity bill will be zero
 vahiin 200 se 400 unit tak kharch karne par aapako bijli ke bilon par 50 fisadi dilli sarkaar dwaara sabsidi milti he
 According to the Delhi government, there are more than two-third consumers in the capital who directly benefit from the subsidy of electricity
 desh ke duusare rajyon main bijli kaa haldilli main 400 unit tak bijli kaa bill kharch karne par aapkaa bill 1,075 rupee aata he, jabaki noida main utani hi maatra main bijli kaa bill 2,123 rupee aata he yani lagbhag do guna
 In Mumbai, the financial capital of the country, you have to pay three times more than Rs 3,000 for the cost of electricity
 karnataka or punjab main bhi 400 unit tak bijli ke kharch par aapako 3,000 rupee se zyada adaa karne padate hai

 nomaharashtra, punjab, karnataka or madhya pradesh main bhi bijli ke bill kaa karant aapako yah sochane par majaboor karegaa ki kaash ham dilli main hote

 tippaniyan Harbhajan Singh (0) could not even open an account
 bhajji ke out hone ke baad 491 ranon ke kul yoga par bharat ne kohli (34) kaa wicket ganvaaya
 Kohli hit three fours in his 93-ball controlled innings
 apni is pari ke dauraan do ran banane ke saath kohli ne test maichon main 1000 ran puure kiye
 Kohli achieved this position in the 27th innings of the 16th Test of his career
 bharat kaa antim wicket bhubaneshwar kumaar (10) ke rup main gira
 With this, tea time was announced
 chennai main 12 wicket lekar bharat kii jeet ke hero rahe ravichandran aswin ne to do wicket lekar iske sanket bhi de die hai
 It is now to be seen how bravely the Australian batsmen can withstand the swing of Bhuvneshwar Kumar, who took three wickets in the first innings along with the spin of Ashwin, Harbhajan Singh and Ravindra Jadeja
 baharhaal, din kii samaapti tak aswin ne david warner (26) or phil huge (0) ko chalata kar diya tha
 Warner hit three fours and a six in a 56-ball fast innings
 warner kaa wicket 56 ke kul yoga par gira or isi yoga par huge bhi out hue
 Opener Ed Cowan returned unbeaten on 26 while Shane Watson has scored nine runs
 watson ne 27 gendon par ek chakka lagaaya he
 Cowan has hit four boundaries in his 100-ball controlled innings
 isse pehle, bhartiya team ne apni pehali pari main 503 ran banaae
 Cheteshwar Pujara (204) and Murali Vijay (167) played brilliant century innings for India
 is tarah bharat ne pehali pari kii tulana main 266 ranon kii mahatvapurn badhat hasil kii
 Glenn Maxwell, playing his first Test for Australia, took four wickets while Xavier Dorthy took three wickets
 james patinson ko do safalataa mili
 Peter Siddle also got one wicket
 bharat ne duusare din ravivaar ko stamps tak ek wicket ke nuksaan par 311 ran banaae the
 The Indian innings started on the third day by Murali (129) and Pujara (162)
 murali ne sanyam ke saath khelte hue test maichon main apane sarvocch yoga (139) ko paar kiya lekin 387 ranon ke kul yoga par vah maxwell kii gend par aid kowan ke haathon lapke gaye
 Murali hit 23 fours and two sixes in his 361-ball marathon innings
 murali or pujaara ne duusare wicket ke liye ricard 370 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 Sachin Tendulkar came on the wicket after Murali was dismissed
 sachin kii maujuudagi main hi pujaara ne apane kariyar kaa doosraa doharaa shatak puraa kiya
 Pujara had earlier played an unbeaten innings of 206 runs against England in Ahmedabad in 2010
 apni is pari ke dauraan pujaara ne test maichon main 1000 ran bhi puure kiye
 Pujara achieved this position in the 18th innings of the 11th Test of his career
 pari kii sankhya ke lihaaj se vah 1000 ran banane vaale duusare sabase tej bhartiya hai jabaki test maichon ke lihaaj se vah is mukaam par sabase tej pahunchane vaale bhartiya khilaadi hai
 Vinod Kambli is the Indian to score 1000 runs in the lowest innings in Tests
 kambali ne 12 maichon kii 14 pariyon main yah mukaam hasil kar liya tha
 As far as achieving this position in the lowest Test matches, the record before Pujara was in the name of Sunil Gavaskar, who scored 1000 runs in 21 innings of 11 matches
 sachin or pujaara kaaphi acchhee ballebaaji kar rahe the lekin 393 ranon ke kul yoga par pujaara ne james patinson kii ek oonchi uthati gend ko hook karne kaa prayaas kiya or jevier dorthi ke haathon lapke gaye
 Pujara hit 30 fours and a six in his 341-ball innings
 sachin lay main the lekin iske baavjood vah saat ran banaakar 404 ranon ke kul yoga par bhojankaal ke thik baad patinson kii gend par wicket ke peeche mathew vade ke haathon lapke gaye
 India's fifth wicket fell as captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni (44)
 dhoni ne apni 43 gendon kii pari main aath chauke lagaae
 Dhoni, who scored a brilliant double century in the second innings of the Chennai Test, shared a 56-run partnership for the fifth wicket with Kohli
 gend ke saath kamaal dikhaa chuke rabindra jadeja (10) ne niraash kiya
 Similarly, Ravichandran Ashwin (1) was out cheaply
 tippaniyan Harbhajan Singh (0) could not even open an account

 australia kii ore se apana pehla test khel rahe glen maxwell ne chaar wicket liye jabaki jevier dorthi ne teen wicket hasil kiye
 James Pattinson had two successes
 ek wicket peter sidle ko bhi mila
 India had scored 311 runs for the loss of one wicket till stumps on the second day on Sunday
 tisare din bhartiya pari kii shuruyaat murali (129) or pujaara (162) ne kii
 Playing with restraint, Murali surpassed his highest total in Test matches (139) but he was caught by Max Cowell at the hands of Ed Cowan for a total of 387 runs
 murali ne apni 361 gendon kii marathon pari main 23 chauke or do chakke lagaae
 Murali and Pujara shared a record 370 runs for the second wicket
 murali ke out hone ke baad sachin tendulkar wicket par aae
 It was in Sachin's presence that Pujara completed his second double century of his career
 pujaara ne isse pehle 2010 main ahmedabad main england ke khilaaf 206 ranon kii naabad pari kheli thi
 During his innings, Pujara also completed 1000 runs in Test matches
 pujaara ne apane kariyar ke 11wein test kii 18veen pari main yah mukaam hasil kiya he
 He is the second fastest Indian to score 1000 runs in terms of innings while he is the fastest Indian to reach this point in terms of Test matches
 test maichon main sabase kam pariyon main 1000 ran banane vaale bhartiya vinod kambali hai
 Kambli achieved this position in 14 innings of 12 matches
 jahaan tak sabase kam test maichon main yah mukaam hasil karne kii baat he to pujaara se pehle yah ricard sunil gavaskar ke naam tha, jinhone 11 maichon kii 21 pariyon main 1000 ran banaae the
 Sachin and Pujara were batting very well but at a total of 393 runs, Pujara attempted to hook a high rising ball from James Pattinson and was caught by Xavier Dorthy
 pujaara ne apni 341 gendon kii pari main 30 chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Sachin was in rhythm but despite this, he scored seven runs and was caught by Matthew Wade on the back of the wicket off Pattinson, just after lunch on a total of 404 runs
 bharat kaa paanchvaan wicket captain mahendra singh dhoni (44) ke rup main gira
 Dhoni hit eight fours in his 43-ball innings
 chennai test kii duusari pari main shandaar doharaa shatak lagane vaale dhoni ne kohli ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 56 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 Ravindra Jadeja (10), who has done wonders with the ball, disappointed
 isi tarah ravichandran aswin (1) saste main out hue
